The breakfast was OK, with a rich variety of varieties, and there were freshly made Taizhou snacks such as Qingtuan and dried vegetable cakes.
Parking is free, the venue is very empty, and the location is much more convenient than Fangyuan. Overall, it is still good, with an old money style.

msg:First of all, the location of the hotel is very good, just next to the Civic Square, and the museum is also nearby. You can basically get there within half an hour by taxi from the two train stations.
But the civic square is really too noisy. There will be singing and dancing in the morning and evening. The sound is very loud. We live in a room near the civic square. When we checked in, the front desk mentioned that it would be a bit noisy. I didn't expect it to be true. Fortunately, after ten o'clock in the evening It's quiet, the influence of late sleepers is not too big, so I'm not happy to change the room. It's understandable that the hotel can't intervene in the external environment. It is recommended that the room can be replaced with soundproof glass or provide anti-noise earplugs. After all, not all guests can bear this disco Same level of noise.
The decoration of the room is relatively old-fashioned, with no bright spots. The soap for washing hands was not provided when you checked in, but there is a soap holder in the bathroom. We only sent the soap after calling, and hope that it will be ready before the guests check in.
There are not many options for breakfast in the hotel. The omelette place says that you can make omelets, but the actual brother said that you canâ€™t make them without ingredients. This experience is not very good. Many hotel buffet breakfasts can make omelets. This hotel is known as a luxury hotel in Taizhou , but misnamed.
Letâ€™s talk about the food delivery service, it says itâ€™s available before 24 oâ€™clock at the latest, but we called to order food at around 23:15 in the evening, but we were told that it was fully booked, and there was not enough manpower to deliver it. In the end, we ordered takeaway. Don't write so late.
OK, all of the above are passable. The most outrageous thing is that the do not disturb button is pressed in the room, but the housekeeper still comes in to clean it. It happened when we went down to have breakfast. We planned to come up after eating to pack up our things and then ask the cleaning to clean up after we went out, so we pressed Do Not Disturb to go to have breakfast. Unexpectedly, when we finished eating, the cleaning came up at the door and said that the room had been cleaned. Alrightâ€¦â€¦â€¦ So the Do Not Disturb button is fake? I can't imagine that if the guest is still sleeping at this time and the door is not locked with an anti-theft chain, wouldn't the cleaning lady just swipe the card to come in? The awareness of hotel safety management is very poor. I have stayed in various hotels, and there has never been any incident of staff entering the room under the condition of do not disturb. I hope the hotel will strengthen management. Of course, the room must be cleaned, but guests must be respected first.
Summary: The hotel is really average, and it is not recommended to choose it if you have quality requirements.
